#[\Attribute] validation should error on trait/interface/enum/abstract class
### Description

See https://3v4l.org/99PhY
```php
<?php

#[Attribute]
enum DemoEnum {}

#[Attribute]
trait DemoTrait {}

#[Attribute]
abstract class DemoAbstract {}

#[Attribute]
interface DemoInterface {}

#[DemoEnum]
#[DemoTrait]
#[DemoAbstract]
#[DemoInterface]
function usesWrongAttrib() {}

$r = new ReflectionFunction( 'usesWrongAttrib' );
$a = $r->getAttributes();
var_dump( $a );
foreach ( $a as $attrib ) {
    try {
        $attrib->newInstance();
    } catch ( Error $e ) {
        echo get_class( $e ) . ": " . $e->getMessage() . "\n";
    }
}
```

    72	static void validate_allow_dynamic_properties(
    73	                zend_attribute *attr, uint32_t target, zend_class_entry *scope)
    74	{
    75	        if (scope->ce_flags & ZEND_ACC_TRAIT) {
    76	                zend_error_noreturn(E_ERROR, "Cannot apply #[\\AllowDynamicProperties] to trait %s",
    77	                        ZSTR_VAL(scope->name)
    78	                );
    79	        }
    80	        if (scope->ce_flags & ZEND_ACC_INTERFACE) {
    81	                zend_error_noreturn(E_ERROR, "Cannot apply #[\\AllowDynamicProperties] to interface %s",
    82	                        ZSTR_VAL(scope->name)
    83	                );
    84	        }
    85	        if (scope->ce_flags & ZEND_ACC_READONLY_CLASS) {
    86	                zend_error_noreturn(E_ERROR, "Cannot apply #[\\AllowDynamicProperties] to readonly class %s",
    87	                        ZSTR_VAL(scope->name)
    88	                );
    89	        }
    90	        if (scope->ce_flags & ZEND_ACC_ENUM) {
    91	                zend_error_noreturn(E_ERROR, "Cannot apply #[\\AllowDynamicProperties] to enum %s",
    92	                        ZSTR_VAL(scope->name)
    93	                );
    94	        }
    95	        scope->ce_flags |= ZEND_ACC_ALLOW_DYNAMIC_PROPERTIES;
    96	}

  7450	static bool zend_is_valid_default_value(zend_type type, zval *value)
  7451	{
  7452	        ZEND_ASSERT(ZEND_TYPE_IS_SET(type));
  7453	        if (ZEND_TYPE_CONTAINS_CODE(type, Z_TYPE_P(value))) {

static void validate_attribute_attribute(
		zend_attribute *attr, uint32_t target, zend_class_entry *scope)
{

static void validate_attribute_attribute(
		zend_attribute *attr, uint32_t target, zend_class_entry *scope)
{
	if (scope->ce_flags & (ZEND_ACC_TRAIT | ZEND_ACC_INTERFACE | ZEND_ACC_ENUM | ZEND_ACC_EXPLICIT_ABSTRACT_CLASS | ZEND_ACC_IMPLICIT_ABSTRACT_CLASS)) {

static void validate_attribute_attribute(
		zend_attribute *attr, uint32_t target, zend_class_entry *scope)
{
	if (scope->ce_flags & (ZEND_ACC_TRAIT | ZEND_ACC_INTERFACE | ZEND_ACC_ENUM | ZEND_ACC_EXPLICIT_ABSTRACT_CLASS | ZEND_ACC_IMPLICIT_ABSTRACT_CLASS)) {
		zend_error_noreturn(E_COMPILE_ERROR, "Cannot use #[Attribute] on %s %s",
			zend_get_object_type(scope), ZSTR_VAL(scope->name)
		);
	}
}

}

static void validate_attribute_attribute(
		zend_attribute *attr, uint32_t target, zend_class_entry *scope)
{
	if (scope->ce_flags & (ZEND_ACC_TRAIT | ZEND_ACC_INTERFACE | ZEND_ACC_ENUM | ZEND_ACC_EXPLICIT_ABSTRACT_CLASS | ZEND_ACC_IMPLICIT_ABSTRACT_CLASS)) {
		zend_error_noreturn(E_COMPILE_ERROR, "Cannot use #[Attribute] on %s %s",
			zend_get_object_type(scope), ZSTR_VAL(scope->name)
		);
	}
}

path = 'Zend/zend_attributes.c'
with open(path, 'r') as f:
    lines = f.readlines()

new_lines = []
for line in lines:
    new_lines.append(line)
    if 'scope->ce_flags |= ZEND_ACC_ALLOW_DYNAMIC_PROPERTIES;' in line:
        new_lines.append('}\n')
        new_lines.append('\n')
        new_lines.append('static void validate_attribute_attribute(\n')
        new_lines.append('\t\tzend_attribute *attr, uint32_t target, zend_class_entry *scope)\n')
        new_lines.append('{\n')
        new_lines.append('\tif (scope->ce_flags & (ZEND_ACC_TRAIT | ZEND_ACC_INTERFACE | ZEND_ACC_ENUM | ZEND_ACC_EXPLICIT_ABSTRACT_CLASS | ZEND_ACC_IMPLICIT_ABSTRACT_CLASS)) {\n')
        new_lines.append('\t\tzend_error_noreturn(E_COMPILE_ERROR, "Cannot use #[Attribute] on %s %s",\n')
        new_lines.append('\t\t\tzend_get_object_type(scope), ZSTR_VAL(scope->name)\n')
        new_lines.append('\t\t);\n')
        new_lines.append('\t}\n')
        # The closing brace and ZEND_METHOD(Attribute, __construct) follow.
        # But I added one above. I need to be careful.

# Actually, let's just do a proper search and replace.
with open(path, 'r') as f:
    content = f.read()

to_add = """
static void validate_attribute_attribute(
		zend_attribute *attr, uint32_t target, zend_class_entry *scope)
{
	if (scope->ce_flags & (ZEND_ACC_TRAIT | ZEND_ACC_INTERFACE | ZEND_ACC_ENUM | ZEND_ACC_EXPLICIT_ABSTRACT_CLASS | ZEND_ACC_IMPLICIT_ABSTRACT_CLASS)) {
		zend_error_noreturn(E_COMPILE_ERROR, "Cannot use #[Attribute] on %s %s",
			zend_get_object_type(scope), ZSTR_VAL(scope->name)
		);
	}
}
"""

content = content.replace('scope->ce_flags |= ZEND_ACC_ALLOW_DYNAMIC_PROPERTIES;\n}', 'scope->ce_flags |= ZEND_ACC_ALLOW_DYNAMIC_PROPERTIES;\n}' + to_add)
content = content.replace('\tzend_ce_attribute = register_class_Attribute();\n\tattr = zend_mark_internal_attribute(zend_ce_attribute);\n', '\tzend_ce_attribute = register_class_Attribute();\n\tattr = zend_mark_internal_attribute(zend_ce_attribute);\n\tattr->validator = validate_attribute_attribute;\n')

with open(path, 'w') as f:
    f.write(content)
EOF

# Using a more robust replacement strategy
import re

to_add = """
static void validate_attribute_attribute(
		zend_attribute *attr, uint32_t target, zend_class_entry *scope)
{
	if (scope->ce_flags & (ZEND_ACC_TRAIT | ZEND_ACC_INTERFACE | ZEND_ACC_ENUM | ZEND_ACC_EXPLICIT_ABSTRACT_CLASS | ZEND_ACC_IMPLICIT_ABSTRACT_CLASS)) {
		zend_error_noreturn(E_COMPILE_ERROR, "Cannot use #[Attribute] on %s %s",
			zend_get_object_type(scope), ZSTR_VAL(scope->name)
		);
	}
}
"""

with open(path, 'w') as f:
    f.write(content)
EOF

python3 << 'EOF'
path = 'Zend/zend_attributes.c'
with open(path, 'r') as f:
    lines = f.readlines()

new_lines = []
for line in lines:
    new_lines.append(line)
    if 'scope->ce_flags |= ZEND_ACC_ALLOW_DYNAMIC_PROPERTIES;' in line:
        # Check next line is '}'
        pass
    if 'zend_ce_attribute = register_class_Attribute();' in line:
        pass

# I'll just use a very simple and safe replacement.
content = "".join(lines)
to_add = """
static void validate_attribute_attribute(
		zend_attribute *attr, uint32_t target, zend_class_entry *scope)
{
	if (scope->ce_flags & (ZEND_ACC_TRAIT | ZEND_ACC_INTERFACE | ZEND_ACC_ENUM | ZEND_ACC_EXPLICIT_ABSTRACT_CLASS | ZEND_ACC_IMPLICIT_ABSTRACT_CLASS)) {
		zend_error_noreturn(E_COMPILE_ERROR, "Cannot use #[Attribute] on %s %s",
			zend_get_object_type(scope), ZSTR_VAL(scope->name)
		);
	}
}
"""
content = content.replace('scope->ce_flags |= ZEND_ACC_ALLOW_DYNAMIC_PROPERTIES;\n}', 'scope->ce_flags |= ZEND_ACC_ALLOW_DYNAMIC_PROPERTIES;\n}' + to_add)
content = content.replace('\tzend_ce_attribute = register_class_Attribute();\n\tattr = zend_mark_internal_attribute(zend_ce_attribute);', '\tzend_ce_attribute = register_class_Attribute();\n\tattr = zend_mark_internal_attribute(zend_ce_attribute);\n\tattr->validator = validate_attribute_attribute;')

with open(path, 'w') as f:
    f.write(content)
EOF
